/lib/actions/role.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | 'use server';
 2 | 
 3 | import { cookies } from 'next/headers';
 4 | import { redirect } from 'next/navigation';
 5 | import { verify } from 'jsonwebtoken';
 6 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 7 | import { getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
 8 | import { revalidatePath } from 'next/cache';
 9 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
10 | import log from '../logger';
11 | import { roles } from '../db/schema/tenant';
12 | import { RoleFormSchema } from '../dto/role';
13 | 
14 | interface UserSession {
15 |   tenantId: string;
16 |   userId: number;
17 | }
18 | 
19 | async function getSession() {
20 |   const token = (await cookies()).get('authToken')?.value;
21 |   if (!token) {
22 |     redirect('/login');
23 |   }
24 |   try {
25 |     return verify(token, env.JWT_SECRET) as UserSession;
26 |   } catch (e) {
27 |     log.error({ error: e }, 'Invalid session token');
28 |     redirect('/login');
29 |   }
30 | }
31 | 
32 | export async function getRoles() {
33 |     const session = await getSession();
34 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
35 |     return db.query.roles.findMany();
36 | }
37 | 
38 | export async function upsertRole(data: unknown) {
39 |     const session = await getSession();
40 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
41 | 
42 |     const validatedFields = RoleFormSchema.safeParse(data);
43 | 
44 |     if (!validatedFields.success) {
45 |         return { success: false, message: 'Invalid role data.' };
46 |     }
47 | 
48 |     const { id, name, description } = validatedFields.data;
49 | 
50 |     try {
51 |         if (id) {
52 |             await db.update(roles).set({ name, description }).where(eq(roles.id, id));
53 |         } else {
54 |             await db.insert(roles).values({ name, description });
55 |         }
56 |         revalidatePath('/dashboard/roles');
57 |         revalidatePath('/dashboard/users'); // Also revalidate users page in case roles changed
58 |         return { success: true, message: `Role successfully ${id ? 'updated' : 'created'}.` };
59 |     } catch (error) {
60 |         log.error({ error }, 'Failed to upsert role');
61 |         return { success: false, message: 'Failed to save role.' };
62 |     }
63 | }
64 | 
65 | export async function deleteRole(roleId: number) {
66 |     const session = await getSession();
67 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
68 | 
69 |     try {
70 |         // You might want to add a check here to ensure the role is not in use
71 |         await db.delete(roles).where(eq(roles.id, roleId));
72 |         revalidatePath('/dashboard/roles');
73 |         revalidatePath('/dashboard/users');
74 |         return { success: true, message: 'Role deleted successfully.' };
75 |     } catch (error) {
76 |         log.error({ error, roleId }, 'Failed to delete role');
77 |         return { success: false, message: 'Failed to delete role. It might be in use.' };
78 |     }
79 | }

/lib/actions/settings.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | 'use server';
 2 | 
 3 | import { revalidatePath } from 'next/cache';
 4 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 5 | import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
 6 | import log from '../logger';
 7 | import { getSession } from '../session';
 8 | import { getTenantDb } from '../db';
 9 | import { users } from '../db/schema/tenant';
10 | import { UpdateProfileSchema, UpdatePasswordSchema } from '../dto/settings';
11 | import { logout } from './auth';
12 | 
13 | // Action to update the user's profile information
14 | export async function updateProfileAction(data: unknown) {
15 |     const session = await getSession();
16 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
17 | 
18 |     const validatedFields = UpdateProfileSchema.safeParse(data);
19 |     if (!validatedFields.success) {
20 |         return { success: false, message: "Invalid data provided." };
21 |     }
22 | 
23 |     const { name, email } = validatedFields.data;
24 | 
25 |     try {
26 |         await db.update(users)
27 |             .set({ name, email })
28 |             .where(eq(users.id, session.userId));
29 |         
30 |         revalidatePath('/dashboard/settings');
31 |         return { success: true, message: "Profile updated successfully." };
32 | 
33 |     } catch (error: unknown) {
34 |         if (error instanceof Error && 'code' in error && error.code === '23505') {
35 |             return { success: false, message: "This email is already in use by another account." };
36 |         }
37 |         log.error({ error }, "Failed to update user profile");
38 |         return { success: false, message: "An unexpected error occurred." };
39 |     }
40 | }
41 | 
42 | // Action to update the user's password
43 | export async function updatePasswordAction(data: unknown) {
44 |     const session = await getSession();
45 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
46 | 
47 |     const validatedFields = UpdatePasswordSchema.safeParse(data);
48 |     if (!validatedFields.success) {
49 |         return { success: false, message: "Invalid data provided." };
50 |     }
51 | 
52 |     const { currentPassword, newPassword } = validatedFields.data;
53 | 
54 |     try {
55 |         const user = await db.query.users.findFirst({ where: eq(users.id, session.userId) });
56 |         if (!user) {
57 |             return { success: false, message: "User not found." };
58 |         }
59 | 
60 |         const isPasswordValid = await bcrypt.compare(currentPassword, user.password);
61 |         if (!isPasswordValid) {
62 |             return { success: false, message: "The current password you entered is incorrect." };
63 |         }
64 | 
65 |         const hashedNewPassword = await bcrypt.hash(newPassword, 12);
66 |         await db.update(users)
67 |             .set({ password: hashedNewPassword })
68 |             .where(eq(users.id, session.userId));
69 | 
70 |         return { success: true, message: "Password updated successfully." };
71 | 
72 |     } catch (error) {
73 |         log.error({ error }, "Failed to update user password");
74 |         return { success: false, message: "An unexpected error occurred." };
75 |     }
76 | }
77 | 
78 | // Action to delete the user's own account
79 | export async function deleteAccountAction() {
80 |     const session = await getSession();
81 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
82 | 
83 |     try {
84 |         await db.delete(users).where(eq(users.id, session.userId));
85 |         // After deletion, log the user out and redirect
86 |         await logout();
87 |         return { success: true, message: "Your account has been deleted." };
88 |     } catch (error) {
89 |         log.error({ error, userId: session.userId }, "Failed to delete user account");
90 |         return { success: false, message: "An unexpected error occurred." };
91 |     }
92 | }

/lib/actions/user.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 'use server';
  2 | 
  3 | import { cookies } from 'next/headers';
  4 | import { redirect } from 'next/navigation';
  5 | import { verify } from 'jsonwebtoken';
  6 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
  7 | import { getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
  8 | import { UserFormSchema, type UserFormInput } from '@/lib/dto/user';
  9 | import { users, usersToRoles } from '@/lib/db/schema/tenant';
 10 | import { revalidatePath } from 'next/cache';
 11 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 12 | import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
 13 | import log from '../logger';
 14 | 
 15 | interface UserSession {
 16 |   tenantId: string;
 17 |   userId: number;
 18 | }
 19 | 
 20 | function isDatabaseError(error: unknown): error is { code: string; message: string } {
 21 |     return typeof error === 'object' && error !== null && 'code' in error;
 22 | }
 23 | 
 24 | async function getSession() {
 25 |   const token = (await cookies()).get('authToken')?.value;
 26 |   if (!token) {
 27 |     redirect('/login');
 28 |   }
 29 |   try {
 30 |     return verify(token, env.JWT_SECRET) as UserSession;
 31 |   } catch (e) {
 32 |     log.error({ error: e }, 'Invalid session token');
 33 |     redirect('/login');
 34 |   }
 35 | }
 36 | 
 37 | export async function getUsersWithRoles() {
 38 |     const session = await getSession();
 39 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
 40 |     
 41 |     const usersWithRoles = await db.query.users.findMany({
 42 |         with: {
 43 |             usersToRoles: {
 44 |                 with: {
 45 |                     role: true
 46 |                 }
 47 |             }
 48 |         }
 49 |     });
 50 | 
 51 |     return usersWithRoles.map(user => ({
 52 |        ...user,
 53 |         roles: user.usersToRoles.map(ur => ur.role.name).join(', ')
 54 |     }));
 55 | }
 56 | 
 57 | // The invalid re-export has been removed from here.
 58 | 
 59 | export async function upsertUserAction(data: UserFormInput) {
 60 |     const session = await getSession();
 61 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
 62 | 
 63 |     const { id, name, email, password, roles: roleIdsStr } = data;
 64 |     const roleIds = roleIdsStr.map(Number);
 65 |     
 66 |     try {
 67 |         await db.transaction(async (tx) => {
 68 |             if (id) { // Update existing user
 69 |                 const userToUpdate: { name: string; email: string; password?: string } = { name, email };
 70 |                 if (password) {
 71 |                     const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 12);
 72 |                     userToUpdate.password = hashedPassword;
 73 |                 }
 74 |                 
 75 |                 await tx.update(users).set(userToUpdate).where(eq(users.id, id));
 76 |                 
 77 |                 await tx.delete(usersToRoles).where(eq(usersToRoles.userId, id));
 78 |                 if (roleIds.length > 0) {
 79 |                     await tx.insert(usersToRoles).values(roleIds.map(roleId => ({
 80 |                         userId: id,
 81 |                         roleId: roleId
 82 |                     })));
 83 |                 }
 84 | 
 85 |             } else { // Create new user
 86 |                 if (!password) throw new Error("Password is required for new users.");
 87 |                 
 88 |                 const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 12);
 89 |                 
 90 |                 const [newUser] = await tx.insert(users).values({
 91 |                     name,
 92 |                     email,
 93 |                     password: hashedPassword,
 94 |                 }).returning({ id: users.id });
 95 | 
 96 |                 if (roleIds.length > 0) {
 97 |                     await tx.insert(usersToRoles).values(roleIds.map(roleId => ({
 98 |                         userId: newUser.id,
 99 |                         roleId: roleId
100 |                     })));
101 |                 }
102 |             }
103 |         });
104 |     } catch (error: unknown) {
105 |         log.error({ error }, 'Failed to upsert user');
106 |         if (isDatabaseError(error) && error.code === '23505') {
107 |             return { 
108 |                 success: false, 
109 |                 message: "A user with this email already exists.",
110 |                 errors: { email: ["This email is already in use."] }
111 |             };
112 |         }
113 |         return { success: false, message: "An unexpected error occurred." };
114 |     }
115 | 
116 |     revalidatePath('/dashboard/users');
117 |     return { success: true, message: `User successfully ${id ? 'updated' : 'created'}.` };
118 | }
119 | 
120 | export async function deleteUserAction(userId: number) {
121 |     const session = await getSession();
122 |     const db = await getTenantDb(session.tenantId);
123 | 
124 |     if (userId === session.userId) {
125 |         return { success: false, message: "You cannot delete your own account." };
126 |     }
127 | 
128 |     try {
129 |         await db.delete(users).where(eq(users.id, userId));
130 |         revalidatePath('/dashboard/users');
131 |         return { success: true, message: "User deleted successfully." };
132 |     } catch (error) {
133 |         log.error({ error, userId }, 'Failed to delete user');
134 |         return { success: false, message: "Failed to delete user." };
135 |     }
136 | }


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/lib/crypto.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { createCipheriv, createDecipheriv, scryptSync, randomBytes } from 'crypto';
 2 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 3 | 
 4 | const ALGORITHM = 'aes-256-gcm';
 5 | const IV_LENGTH = 16;
 6 | const TAG_LENGTH = 16;
 7 | const KEY = scryptSync(env.ENCRYPTION_KEY, 'salt', 32);
 8 | 
 9 | export function encrypt(text: string): string {
10 |   const iv = randomBytes(IV_LENGTH);
11 |   const cipher = createCipheriv(ALGORITHM, KEY, iv);
12 |   const encrypted = Buffer.concat([cipher.update(text, 'utf8'), cipher.final()]);
13 |   const tag = cipher.getAuthTag();
14 |   return Buffer.concat([iv, tag, encrypted]).toString('hex');
15 | }
16 | 
17 | export function decrypt(encryptedText: string): string {
18 |   const data = Buffer.from(encryptedText, 'hex');
19 |   const iv = data.slice(0, IV_LENGTH);
20 |   const tag = data.slice(IV_LENGTH, IV_LENGTH + TAG_LENGTH);
21 |   const encrypted = data.slice(IV_LENGTH + TAG_LENGTH);
22 |   const decipher = createDecipheriv(ALGORITHM, KEY, iv);
23 |   decipher.setAuthTag(tag);
24 |   const decrypted = Buffer.concat([decipher.update(encrypted), decipher.final()]);
25 |   return decrypted.toString('utf8');
26 | }


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/lib/db/index.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // lib/db/index.ts
 2 | import { drizzle, NodePgDatabase } from 'drizzle-orm/node-postgres';
 3 | import { Pool } from 'pg';
 4 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 5 | import { tenants } from './schema/shared';
 6 | import * as tenantSchema from './schema/tenant';
 7 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 8 | import { decrypt } from '@/lib/crypto';
 9 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
10 | 
11 | // 1. Main DB Client (for managing tenant metadata)
12 | const mainPool = new Pool({ connectionString: env.POSTGRES_URL });
13 | export const mainDb = drizzle(mainPool, { schema: { tenants } });
14 | 
15 | // 2. Tenant DB Client Cache
16 | const tenantDbCache = new Map<string, NodePgDatabase<typeof tenantSchema>>();
17 | 
18 | // 3. Function to get a tenant-specific DB client
19 | export async function getTenantDb(tenantId: string): Promise<NodePgDatabase<typeof tenantSchema>> {
20 |   if (tenantDbCache.has(tenantId)) {
21 |     log.info({ tenantId }, 'Tenant DB client cache HIT.');
22 |     return tenantDbCache.get(tenantId)!;
23 |   }
24 |   log.info({ tenantId }, 'Tenant DB client cache MISS.');
25 | 
26 |   const results = await mainDb
27 |     .select({ connectionString: tenants.connectionString })
28 |     .from(tenants)
29 |     .where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId))
30 |     .limit(1);
31 | 
32 |   // --- Start of Fix ---
33 |   const tenantData = results[0]; // Access the first element of the array
34 | 
35 |   if (!tenantData) {
36 |     log.error({ tenantId }, 'Tenant not found in main database.');
37 |     throw new Error('Tenant not found');
38 |   }
39 | 
40 |   const decryptedConnectionString = decrypt(tenantData.connectionString);
41 |   // --- End of Fix ---
42 | 
43 |   const tenantPool = new Pool({ connectionString: decryptedConnectionString });
44 |   const tenantDb = drizzle(tenantPool, { schema: tenantSchema });
45 | 
46 |   tenantDbCache.set(tenantId, tenantDb);
47 |   log.info({ tenantId }, 'Created and cached new tenant DB client.');
48 | 
49 |   return tenantDb;
50 | }

/lib/db/migrate.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // In /lib/db/migrate.ts
 2 | import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js';
 3 | import { migrate } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js/migrator';
 4 | import postgres from 'postgres';
 5 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
 6 | 
 7 | export async function runTenantMigrations(connectionString: string) {
 8 |   // Use postgres 'on-the-fly' with max 1 connection for migrations
 9 |   const migrationClient = postgres(connectionString, { max: 1 });
10 |   const db = drizzle(migrationClient);
11 | 
12 |   try {
13 |     log.info('Starting tenant migration...');
14 |     await migrate(db, { migrationsFolder: './drizzle/tenant' }); // Assumes tenant migrations are in 'drizzle/tenant'
15 |     log.info('Tenant migration completed successfully.');
16 |   } catch (error) {
17 |     log.error({ error }, 'Tenant migration failed.');
18 |     // Re-throw the error to ensure the API call fails loudly
19 |     throw new Error('Could not run tenant migrations.');
20 |   } finally {
21 |     // Ensure the connection is closed
22 |     await migrationClient.end();
23 |   }
24 | }

/lib/db/schema/tenant.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { serial, text, pgTable, integer, timestamp, primaryKey } from 'drizzle-orm/pg-core';
 2 | import { relations } from 'drizzle-orm';
 3 | 
 4 | // Existing users table
 5 | export const users = pgTable('users', {
 6 |   id: serial('id').primaryKey(),
 7 |   name: text('name').notNull(),
 8 |   email: text('email').notNull().unique(),
 9 |   password: text('password').notNull(),
10 | });
11 | 
12 | // New roles table
13 | export const roles = pgTable('roles', {
14 |     id: serial('id').primaryKey(),
15 |     name: text('name').notNull().unique(),
16 |     description: text('description'),
17 |     createdAt: timestamp('created_at').defaultNow().notNull(),
18 | });
19 | 
20 | // New users_to_roles join table
21 | export const usersToRoles = pgTable('users_to_roles', {
22 |     userId: integer('user_id').notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),
23 |     roleId: integer('role_id').notNull().references(() => roles.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),
24 | }, (t) => ({
25 |     pk: primaryKey({ columns: [t.userId, t.roleId] }),
26 | }));
27 | 
28 | // --- RELATIONS ---
29 | 
30 | export const usersRelations = relations(users, ({ many }) => ({
31 |     usersToRoles: many(usersToRoles),
32 | }));
33 | 
34 | export const rolesRelations = relations(roles, ({ many }) => ({
35 |     usersToRoles: many(usersToRoles),
36 | }));
37 | 
38 | export const usersToRolesRelations = relations(usersToRoles, ({ one }) => ({
39 |     role: one(roles, {
40 |         fields: [usersToRoles.roleId],
41 |         references: [roles.id],
42 |     }),
43 |     user: one(users, {
44 |         fields: [usersToRoles.userId],
45 |         references: [users.id],
46 |     }),
47 | }));

/lib/dto/user.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { z } from 'zod';
 2 | 
 3 | export const UserFormSchema = z.object({
 4 |   id: z.number().optional(),
 5 |   name: z.string().min(2, { message: 'Name must be at least 2 characters.' }),
 6 |   email: z.string().email({ message: 'Please enter a valid email.' }),
 7 |   password: z.string().optional(),
 8 |   roles: z.array(z.string()).min(1, { message: 'At least one role must be selected.' }),
 9 | }).refine(data => {
10 |     // If it's a new user (no id), password must be a string of at least 8 chars.
11 |     if (!data.id) {
12 |         return !!data.password && data.password.length >= 8;
13 |     }
14 |     // If it's an existing user and a password IS provided, it must be at least 8 chars.
15 |     // If no password is provided for an existing user, it's valid (means no change).
16 |     if (data.id && data.password) {
17 |         return data.password.length >= 8;
18 |     }
19 |     return true;
20 | }, {
21 |     message: "Password must be at least 8 characters.",
22 |     path: ["password"], // Point the error to the password field
23 | });
24 | 
25 | export type UserFormInput = z.infer<typeof UserFormSchema>;

/lib/neon/api.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // In lib/neon/api.ts
 2 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 3 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
 4 | 
 5 | const NEON_API_BASE = 'https://console.neon.tech/api/v2';
 6 | 
 7 | export async function createNeonProject(tenantId: string) {
 8 |   log.info({ tenantId }, '[NeonAPI] Starting project creation process.');
 9 | 
10 |   const headers = {
11 |     'Authorization': `Bearer ${env.NEON_API_KEY}`,
12 |     'Content-Type': 'application/json',
13 |     'Accept': 'application/json',
14 |   };
15 | 
16 |   const projectResponse = await fetch(`${NEON_API_BASE}/projects`, {
17 |     method: 'POST',
18 |     headers,
19 |     body: JSON.stringify({
20 |       project: { name: `edux-tenant-${tenantId}` },
21 |     }),
22 |   });
23 | 
24 |   if (!projectResponse.ok) {
25 |     const errorBody = await projectResponse.text();
26 |     log.error({ tenantId, status: projectResponse.status, errorBody }, '[NeonAPI] Failed to create project.');
27 |     throw new Error(`Failed to create Neon project: ${errorBody}`);
28 |   }
29 | 
30 |   const responseData = await projectResponse.json();
31 |   const project = responseData.project;
32 |   const connectionDetails = responseData.connection_uris?.[0];
33 |   const connection_uri = connectionDetails?.connection_uri;
34 | 
35 |   if (!connection_uri) {
36 |     log.error({ responseData }, '[NeonAPI] Connection URI could not be extracted from the response.');
37 |     throw new Error('Connection URI could not be extracted from the Neon API response.');
38 |   }
39 | 
40 |   log.info({ tenantId, projectId: project.id }, '[NeonAPI] Project created successfully.');
41 | 
42 |   // The modification to create a pooled string has been removed.
43 |   // We will now return the original, direct connection string.
44 | 
45 |   return {
46 |     projectId: project.id,
47 |     connectionString: connection_uri,
48 |   };
49 | }

/lib/session.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { cookies } from 'next/headers';
 2 | import { redirect } from 'next/navigation';
 3 | import { verify } from 'jsonwebtoken';
 4 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 5 | import log from './logger';
 6 | 
 7 | export interface UserSession {
 8 |   tenantId: string;
 9 |   userId: number;
10 |   email: string;
11 |   name: string;
12 | }
13 | 
14 | /**
15 |  * Retrieves the session from the auth token cookie.
16 |  * Redirects to '/login' if the token is missing or invalid.
17 |  * This function should be used in Server Components and Server Actions to protect routes.
18 |  * @returns {Promise<UserSession>} The decoded user session.
19 |  */
20 | export async function getSession(): Promise<UserSession> {
21 |   const token = (await cookies()).get('authToken')?.value;
22 | 
23 |   if (!token) {
24 |     redirect('/login');
25 |   }
26 | 
27 |   try {
28 |     // Verify the token and return the session payload
29 |     const session = verify(token, env.JWT_SECRET) as UserSession;
30 |     return session;
31 |   } catch (e) {
32 |     log.error({ error: e }, 'Invalid session token. Redirecting to login.');
33 |     // If verification fails, redirect to login
34 |     redirect('/login');
35 |   }
36 | }

/middleware.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 2 | import logger from './lib/logger';
 3 | 
 4 | // Extracts the tenant ID from the hostname.
 5 | const getTenantId = (host: string): string | null => {
 6 |   const parts = host.split('.');
 7 | 
 8 |   // Handles tenant.localhost:3000 in development
 9 |   if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' && parts.length === 2 && parts[1].startsWith('localhost')) {
10 |     return parts[0];
11 |   }
12 | 
13 |   // Handles tenant.example.com in production
14 |   if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && parts.length > 1 && parts[0] !== 'www') {
15 |     return parts[0];
16 |   }
17 | 
18 |   return null;
19 | };
20 | 
21 | 
22 | export function middleware(request: NextRequest) {
23 |   const host = request.headers.get('host') || '';
24 |   const tenantId = getTenantId(host);
25 |   const { pathname } = request.nextUrl;
26 |   const log = logger.child({ tenantId, pathname });
27 | 
28 |   log.info('Middleware processing request');
29 | 
30 |   console.log('Incoming cookies:', request.cookies.getAll());
31 |   console.log('TenantId:', tenantId, 'Pathname:', pathname);
32 | 
33 |   const headers = new Headers(request.headers);
34 |   if (tenantId) {
35 |     headers.set('x-tenant-id', tenantId);
36 |   }
37 | 
38 |   // Allow public routes regardless of tenant.
39 |   if (pathname === '/' || pathname === '/signup') {
40 |     return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
41 |   }
42 | 
43 |   // If on a tenant subdomain, allow access to login.
44 |   if (tenantId && pathname.startsWith('/login')) {
45 |       return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
46 |   }
47 | 
48 |   // All API routes are allowed to pass through for now;
49 |   // authentication will be handled at the route level.
50 |   if (pathname.startsWith('/api')) {
51 |     return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
52 |   }
53 | 
54 |   // For dashboard access, check for an auth token.
55 |   const token = request.cookies.get('authToken');
56 |   if (pathname.startsWith('/dashboard') && !token) {
57 |     log.warn('Access to dashboard denied without token, redirecting to login.');
58 |     const loginUrl = new URL('/login', request.url);
59 |     return NextResponse.redirect(loginUrl);
60 |   }
61 | 
62 |   return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
63 | }
64 | 
65 | export const config = {
66 |   matcher: [
67 |     /*
68 |      * Match all request paths except for the ones starting with:
69 |      * - _next/static (static files)
70 |      * - _next/image (image optimization files)
71 |      * - favicon.ico (favicon file)
72 |      */
73 |     '/((?!_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico).*)',
74 |   ],
75 | };

/scripts/migrate-tenant.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // Create a new file: /scripts/migrate-tenant.ts
 2 | import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js';
 3 | import { migrate } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js/migrator';
 4 | import postgres from 'postgres';
 5 | import 'dotenv/config';
 6 | 
 7 | async function main() {
 8 |   const connectionString = process.env.TENANT_DATABASE_URL;
 9 | 
10 |   if (!connectionString) {
11 |     throw new Error('TENANT_DATABASE_URL environment variable is not set.');
12 |   }
13 | 
14 |   // Use postgres 'on-the-fly' with max 1 connection for migrations
15 |   const migrationClient = postgres(connectionString, { max: 1 });
16 |   const db = drizzle(migrationClient);
17 | 
18 |   console.log('Running migrations for tenant...');
19 | 
20 |   await migrate(db, { migrationsFolder: './drizzle/tenant' });
21 | 
22 |   console.log('Migrations completed successfully.');
23 | 
24 |   await migrationClient.end();
25 |   process.exit(0);
26 | }
27 | 
28 | main().catch((err) => {
29 |   console.error('Migration failed:', err);
30 |   process.exit(1);
31 | });
